# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="dbc66-105">Veraltete Member in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dbc66-106">In diesem Artikel werden die Typmember aufgeführt, die in .NET Framework 4.5 und höheren Versionen veraltet sind.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dbc66-107">Typmember werden nach Assembly gruppiert.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dbc66-108">In diesem Artikel werden die Member veralteter Typen nicht aufgeführt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dbc66-109">Eine Liste veralteter Typen finden Sie unter [Veraltete Typen](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

> |<xref:Microsoft.VisualBasic.MyServices.RegistryProxy?displayProperty=nameWithType>|<xref:Microsoft.VisualBasic.MyServices.RegistryProxy.DynData%2A>|<span data-ttu-id="dbc66-1184">Der Registrierungsschlüssel `DynData` funktioniert nur unter Win9x, was von dieser .NET Framework-Version nicht unterstützt wird.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-1184">The `DynData` registry key works only on Win9x, which isn't supported by this version of the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dbc66-1185">Verwenden Sie stattdessen den Registrierungsschlüssel `PerformanceData`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-1185">Use the `PerformanceData` registry key instead.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dbc66-1186">Diese Eigenschaft wird in einer der nächsten Framework-Versionen entfernt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dbc66-1186">This property will be removed from a future version of the Framework.</span></span>|
